27   * @summary Test corner cases of sin and cos

34  public class SinCosCornerCasesTests {
35      private SinCosCornerCasesTests() {throw new AssertionError("No instances for you.");}

37      public static void main(String... args) {
38          int failures = 0;
39  
40  
41          failures += testCornerCasesSin();

47          }

1503     private static int testSinCase(double input, double bound1, double bound2) {
1504         int failures = 0;
1505         failures += Tests.testBounds("Math.sin", input, Math.sin(input), bound1, bound2);
1506         return failures;
1507     }

2922     private static int testCosCase(double input, double bound1, double bound2) {
